import urllib.request, json, os, sys

API_KEY = os.environ.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY", "")
ENDPOINT = "https://app-crlrq8qvf8jl-api-zYm4ze3j7XvL.gateway.appmedo.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:streamGenerateContent?alt=sse"

def search(query):
    payload = json.dumps({"contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": query}]}]}).encode()
    req = urllib.request.Request(ENDPOINT, data=payload, headers={
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        "X-Gateway-Authorization": f"Bearer {API_KEY}"
    })
    text = ""
    try:
        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=60) as r:
            buf = ""
            for chunk in r:
                buf += chunk.decode("utf-8", errors="replace")
                for line in buf.split("\n"):
                    if line.startswith("data: "):
                        d = line[6:].strip()
                        if d == "[DONE]": continue
                        try:
                            j = json.loads(d)
                            text += j.get("candidates",[{}])[0].get("content",{}).get("parts",[{}])[0].get("text","")
                        except: pass
                buf = buf.split("\n")[-1]
    except Exception as e:
        return f"ERROR: {e}"
    return text

import urllib.request, json, os

API_KEY = os.environ.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY", "")
ENDPOINT = "https://app-crlrq8qvf8jl-api-zYm4ze3j7XvL.gateway.appmedo.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:streamGenerateContent?alt=sse"

def search(query):
    payload = json.dumps({"contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": query}]}]}).encode()
    req = urllib.request.Request(ENDPOINT, data=payload, headers={
        "Content-Type": "application/json", "X-Gateway-Authorization": f"Bearer {API_KEY}"
    })
    text = ""
    try:
        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=60) as r:
            buf = ""
            for chunk in r:
                buf += chunk.decode("utf-8", errors="replace")
                for line in buf.split("\n"):
                    if line.startswith("data: "):
                        d = line[6:].strip()
                        if d == "[DONE]": continue
                        try:
                            j = json.loads(d)
                            text += j.get("candidates",[{}])[0].get("content",{}).get("parts",[{}])[0].get("text","")
                        except: pass
                buf = buf.split("\n")[-1]
    except Exception as e:
        return f"ERROR: {e}"
    return text

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

CLOSE_PATS = ('    },', '      },')

updated = 0
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    m = re.match(r'^( {6}| {8})id:\s*[\'`]([^\'`]+)', line)
    if not m: continue
    sid = m.group(2)
    if sid not in SONG_ID_MAP: continue
    new_id = SONG_ID_MAP[sid]
    # Find and replace the existing youtubeId in this song block
    n = len(m.group(1))
    cp = CLOSE_PATS[0] if n == 6 else CLOSE_PATS[1]
    for j in range(i+1, min(i+70, len(lines))):
        if re.match(r'^\s+youtubeId:', lines[j]):
            old = lines[j]
            lines[j] = re.sub(r"youtubeId:\s*'[^']*'", f"youtubeId: '{new_id}'", lines[j])
            if lines[j] != old:
                print(f"✓ {sid}: → {new_id}")
                updated += 1
            break
        if lines[j].rstrip() in CLOSE_PATS: break

print(f"\nUpdated: {updated} songs")
with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    f.writelines(lines)

COMMAND:
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import re, collections

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Extract artist context too
artist_blocks = re.split(r'\n  \{', content)
song_info = []  # (yt_id, song_id, song_title, artist_name)

# Parse more carefully: get artist name + song data
current_artist = None
for m in re.finditer(r"name:\s*['\"`]([^'\"` ][^'\"` ]*(?:\s+[^'\"` ]+)*?)['\"`]", content):
    pass  # skip, use different approach

# Extract structured: artist_id, artist_name, song_id, song_title, youtube_id
pattern = re.compile(
    r'id:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`][^{]*?name:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`].*?songs:.*?\[',
    re.DOTALL
)
song_pattern = re.compile(
    r'(?:^|\n)( {6}| {8})id:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`].*?title:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`].*?youtubeId:\s*\'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})\'',
    re.DOTALL
)

# Simpler: get all song blocks with context
all_songs = []
for m in re.finditer(r"(?m)^(  \{[^{]*?id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`]+)['\"`][^{]*?name:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`]+)['\"`])", content, re.DOTALL):
    pass

# Use grep-style approach
lines = content.split('\n')
current_artist_name = None
current_artist_id = None
in_songs = False
i = 0
while i < len(lines):
    line = lines[i]
    # Detect artist-level id (2-space indent)
    m2 = re.match(r'^  id:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`]', line)
    if m2:
        current_artist_id = m2.group(1)
        in_songs = False
    m2n = re.match(r'^  name:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`]', line)
    if m2n:
        current_artist_name = m2n.group(1)
    if 'songs:' in line and line.strip().startswith('songs'):
        in_songs = True
    # Song-level id (6 or 8 spaces)
    if in_songs:
        ms = re.match(r'^( {6}| {8})id:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`]', line)
        if ms:
            sid = ms.group(2)
            # find title and youtubeId in next ~30 lines
            title = None; yt_id = None
            for j in range(i+1, min(i+35, len(lines))):
                mt = re.match(r"^[^\S\n]*title:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`]+)['\"`]", lines[j])
                my = re.match(r"^[^\S\n]*youtubeId:\s*'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})'", lines[j])
                if mt and not title: title = mt.group(1)
                if my and not yt_id: yt_id = my.group(1)
                if title and yt_id: break
            if yt_id:
                all_songs.append((current_artist_id, current_artist_name, sid, title or sid, yt_id))
    i += 1

# Group by youtube_id
by_yt = collections.defaultdict(list)
for artist_id, artist_name, sid, title, yt_id in all_songs:
    by_yt[yt_id].append((artist_id, artist_name, sid, title))

# Still-shared IDs (2+ songs using same ID = likely placeholder)
print("=== Still-shared YouTube IDs (2+ songs) ===")
total_needs_fix = 0
for yt_id, songs in sorted(by_yt.items(), key=lambda x: -len(x[1])):
    if len(songs) >= 2:
        total_needs_fix += len(songs) - 1  # first occurrence might be correct
        print(f"\n{yt_id} ({len(songs)} songs):")
        for aid, aname, sid, title in songs:
            print(f"  [{aname}] {title} ({sid})")

print(f"\nTotal songs needing unique IDs: ~{total_needs_fix}")
print(f"Total unique placeholder IDs: {sum(1 for v in by_yt.values() if len(v)>=2)}")
PYEOF

import re, collections

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts') as f:
    content = f.read()

lines = content.split('\n')
current_artist_name = None
current_artist_id = None
in_songs = False
all_songs = []
i = 0
while i < len(lines):
    line = lines[i]
    m2 = re.match(r'^  id:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`]', line)
    if m2: current_artist_id = m2.group(1); in_songs = False
    m2n = re.match(r'^  name:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`]', line)
    if m2n: current_artist_name = m2n.group(1)
    if re.match(r'^  songs:', line): in_songs = True
    if re.match(r'^  connections:|^  x:|^  bio:|^  image:', line): in_songs = False
    if in_songs:
        ms = re.match(r'^( {6}| {8})id:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`]', line)
        if ms:
            sid = ms.group(2)
            title = None; yt_id = None
            for j in range(i+1, min(i+35, len(lines))):
                mt = re.match(r"^[^\S\n]*title:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`]+)['\"`]", lines[j])
                my = re.match(r"^[^\S\n]*youtubeId:\s*'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})'", lines[j])
                if mt and not title: title = mt.group(1)
                if my and not yt_id: yt_id = my.group(1)
                if title and yt_id: break
            if yt_id:
                all_songs.append((current_artist_id, current_artist_name, sid, title or sid, yt_id))
    i += 1

by_yt = collections.defaultdict(list)
for aid, aname, sid, title, yt_id in all_songs:
    by_yt[yt_id].append((aid, aname, sid, title))

# Build search queries for all shared IDs
# Group songs by artist for AI queries
queries_needed = []
for yt_id, songs in sorted(by_yt.items(), key=lambda x: -len(x[1])):
    if len(songs) >= 2:
        for aid, aname, sid, title in songs[1:]:  # skip first (likely the original)
            queries_needed.append((aid, aname, sid, title, yt_id))

print(f"Total songs needing new IDs: {len(queries_needed)}")
print("\n-- Batch AI search queries --")
# Group into batches of 7
batch = []
for item in queries_needed:
    batch.append(item)
    
# Print first 50 for verification
for aid, aname, sid, title, yt_id in queries_needed[:50]:
    print(f"  [{aname}] '{title}' (song-id: {sid}) currently: {yt_id}")

python3 << 'PYEOF'
import re, collections

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Split by top-level artist objects
# Each artist block starts at "  {" at column 2
artist_chunks = re.split(r'\n  \{', content)
all_songs = []

for chunk in artist_chunks[1:]:  # skip file header
    # Extract artist name and id
    aname_m = re.search(r"name:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`]+)['\"`]", chunk)
    aid_m   = re.search(r"^id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`]+)['\"`]", chunk, re.MULTILINE)
    if not aname_m or not aid_m: continue
    aname = aname_m.group(1)
    aid   = aid_m.group(1)
    
    # Extract songs section
    songs_m = re.search(r'songs:\s*\[(.*?)\],?\s*(?:x:|connections:|bio:|image:)', chunk, re.DOTALL)
    if not songs_m: continue
    songs_block = songs_m.group(1)
    
    # Extract individual songs
    for sm in re.finditer(r"id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`]+)['\"`].*?title:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`]+)['\"`].*?youtubeId:\s*'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})'", songs_block, re.DOTALL):
        sid, title, yt_id = sm.group(1), sm.group(2), sm.group(3)
        all_songs.append((aid, aname, sid, title, yt_id))

by_yt = collections.defaultdict(list)
for aid, aname, sid, title, yt_id in all_songs:
    by_yt[yt_id].append((aid, aname, sid, title))

print(f"Total songs parsed: {len(all_songs)}")

# Show shared IDs
print("\n=== Still-shared IDs (2+ songs) ===")
needs_fix = []
for yt_id, songs in sorted(by_yt.items(), key=lambda x: -len(x[1])):
    if len(songs) >= 2:
        print(f"\n{yt_id} ({len(songs)}):")
        for i, (aid, aname, sid, title) in enumerate(songs):
            marker = "OK" if i == 0 else "FIX"
            print(f"  [{marker}] [{aname}] '{title}' ({sid})")
            if i > 0:
                needs_fix.append((aname, title, sid, yt_id))

print(f"\nTotal songs needing new IDs: {len(needs_fix)}")

import re, collections

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts') as f:
    lines = f.readlines()

# Line-by-line state machine
current_artist_name = "Unknown"
current_artist_id = "unknown"
depth = 0  # track brace depth from ARTISTS array start
in_artists = False
in_songs_array = False
song_brace_depth = 0

# Track per-song
cur_song = None

all_songs = []

i = 0
while i < len(lines):
    raw = lines[i]
    stripped = raw.strip()
    
    # Detect ARTISTS array start
    if 'export const ARTISTS' in raw:
        in_artists = True
    
    if not in_artists:
        i += 1
        continue
    
    # Detect artist-level id/name (exactly 2 leading spaces, then id: or name:)
    m_aid = re.match(r'^  id:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`]', raw)
    m_aname = re.match(r'^  name:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`]', raw)
    if m_aid:
        current_artist_id = m_aid.group(1)
        in_songs_array = False
    if m_aname:
        current_artist_name = m_aname.group(1)

    # Detect songs: [ array start
    if re.match(r'^  songs:\s*\[', raw):
        in_songs_array = True
        i += 1
        continue
    
    # Detect end of songs array
    if in_songs_array and re.match(r'^  \],', raw):
        in_songs_array = False
    
    if in_songs_array:
        # Song-level id (6 or 8 spaces)
        ms = re.match(r'^( {6}| {8})id:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`]', raw)
        if ms:
            cur_song = {'artist_id': current_artist_id, 'artist_name': current_artist_name,
                        'song_id': ms.group(2), 'title': None, 'yt_id': None}
        
        if cur_song:
            mt = re.match(r'^[^\S\n]*title:\s*[`\'"]([^`\'"]+)[`\'"]', raw)
            my = re.match(r"^[^\S\n]*youtubeId:\s*'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})'", raw)
            if mt and not cur_song['title']:
                cur_song['title'] = mt.group(1)
            if my and not cur_song['yt_id']:
                cur_song['yt_id'] = my.group(1)
                # Song complete enough
                all_songs.append(dict(cur_song))
                cur_song = None
    
    i += 1

print(f"Parsed: {len(all_songs)} songs")
print(f"Sample: {all_songs[0]}")
print(f"Sample: {all_songs[10]}")

# Group by yt_id
by_yt = collections.defaultdict(list)
for s in all_songs:
    by_yt[s['yt_id']].append(s)

# Show top shared IDs
print("\n=== Top shared IDs ===")
for yt_id, songs in sorted(by_yt.items(), key=lambda x: -len(x[1]))[:15]:
    if len(songs) >= 2:
        print(f"\n{yt_id} ({len(songs)}):")
        for s in songs:
            print(f"  [{s['artist_name']}] '{s['title']}' ({s['song_id']})")

# Fix parser: songs use 6-space indent (not 2-space songs: array marker)
# The structure is actually: songs are inside the artist object with 6-space indented id:
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import re, collections

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts') as f:
    content = f.read()

lines = content.split('\n')

current_artist_name = None
current_artist_id = None
all_songs = []
cur_song = None

for i, raw in enumerate(lines):
    # Artist id/name: exactly 2 spaces + id: or name:
    m_aid = re.match(r'^  id:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`]', raw)
    m_aname = re.match(r'^  name:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`]', raw)
    if m_aid:
        current_artist_id = m_aid.group(1)
        cur_song = None
    if m_aname:
        current_artist_name = m_aname.group(1)

    # Song id: 6-space or 8-space (but NOT album-level which is also 6-space inside albums:[])
    # Key distinction: song id comes AFTER "songs: [" not "albums: ["
    # Simpler: just match 6-space id: and check next lines for youtubeId
    ms = re.match(r'^( {6}| {8})id:\s*[\'`]([^\'\`]+)[\'`]', raw)
    if ms and current_artist_id:
        indent = len(ms.group(1))
        sid = ms.group(2)
        # Look ahead for title and youtubeId before next id:
        title = yt_id = None
        for j in range(i+1, min(i+40, len(lines))):
            nxt = lines[j]
            mt = re.match(r"^[ \t]+title:\s*[`'\"]([^`'\"]+)[`'\"]", nxt)
            my = re.match(r"^[ \t]+youtubeId:\s*'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})'", nxt)
            # Stop at next same-or-lower indent id:
            if re.match(r'^( {6}| {8})id:', nxt) and j > i+1: break
            if re.match(r'^  [a-z]', nxt) and not nxt.strip().startswith('//') and j > i+3: break
            if mt and not title: title = mt.group(1)
            if my and not yt_id: yt_id = my.group(1)
        if yt_id and title:
            all_songs.append({
                'artist_id': current_artist_id,
                'artist_name': current_artist_name,
                'song_id': sid,
                'title': title,
                'yt_id': yt_id
            })

print(f"Total songs parsed: {len(all_songs)}")

# Group by yt_id
by_yt = collections.defaultdict(list)
for s in all_songs:
    by_yt[s['yt_id']].append(s)

needs_fix = []
print("\n=== Shared IDs (2+ songs) ===")
for yt_id, songs in sorted(by_yt.items(), key=lambda x: -len(x[1])):
    if len(songs) >= 2:
        print(f"\n{yt_id} ({len(songs)}):")
        for k, s in enumerate(songs):
            marker = "keep" if k == 0 else "FIX"
            print(f"  [{marker}] [{s['artist_name']}] '{s['title']}' ({s['song_id']})")
            if k > 0:
                needs_fix.append(s)

print(f"\nTotal songs needing unique IDs: {len(needs_fix)}")

import re, collections

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Direct regex: find all youtubeId values and which song/artist they belong to
# Pattern: capture artist name, then song title + youtubeId together
# Use a single findall across the entire file

# Step 1: extract (artist_name, song_id, title, youtubeId) tuples using
# a window-based approach on the raw text
matches = re.findall(
    r"youtubeId:\s*'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})'",
    content
)
print(f"Total youtubeId occurrences: {len(matches)}")
print(f"Unique: {len(set(matches))}")

# Count shared ones
c = collections.Counter(matches)
shared = [(yt, cnt) for yt, cnt in c.most_common() if cnt >= 2]
print(f"\nShared IDs (2+): {len(shared)}")
for yt, cnt in shared[:10]:
    print(f"  {yt}: {cnt}x")

python3 << 'PYEOF'
import re, collections

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Find each song block by locating youtubeId and scanning backward for title/id,
# and also find the containing artist name
# Build a list of (artist_name, song_id, title, yt_id) for SONGS only (not albums)

# Strategy: find all occurrences of youtubeId with context
results = []

for m in re.finditer(r"youtubeId:\s*'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})'", content):
    yt_id = m.group(1)
    pos = m.start()
    window = content[max(0, pos-600):pos]
    
    # Find the last artist name before this position
    anames = re.findall(r"(?:^|\n)  name:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", window)
    aname = anames[-1] if anames else "Unknown"
    
    # Find title in window (last one before youtubeId)
    titles = re.findall(r"(?:^|\n)\s+title:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", window)
    title = titles[-1] if titles else None
    
    # Find song id in window
    sids = re.findall(r"(?:^|\n)[ \t]+id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", window)
    sid = sids[-1] if sids else None
    
    # Skip album-level youtubeIds (they appear on the same line as significance:)
    line_start = content.rfind('\n', 0, pos)
    line = content[line_start:pos+30]
    if 'significance' in line or 'albums' in content[max(0,pos-20):pos+20]:
        continue
    
    results.append((aname, sid, title, yt_id))

print(f"Song-level youtubeIds: {len(results)}")

# Group by yt_id
by_yt = collections.defaultdict(list)
for aname, sid, title, yt_id in results:
    by_yt[yt_id].append((aname, sid, title))

# Build fix list: for each shared ID, all but the first need replacement
needs_fix = []
print("\n=== Shared IDs needing fix ===")
for yt_id, songs in sorted(by_yt.items(), key=lambda x: -len(x[1])):
    if len(songs) >= 2:
        print(f"\n{yt_id} x{len(songs)}:")
        for k, (aname, sid, title) in enumerate(songs):
            tag = "OK " if k==0 else "FIX"
            print(f"  [{tag}] [{aname}] '{title}' ({sid})")
            if k > 0:
                needs_fix.append({'artist': aname, 'song_id': sid, 'title': title, 'current_yt': yt_id})

print(f"\nTotal to fix: {len(needs_fix)}")

COMMAND:
# Get song context with proper artist lookup using position-based scan
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import re, json

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Build: list of (pos, artist_name) for all artist name declarations
artist_positions = []
for m in re.finditer(r'\n  name:\s*[\'"`]([^\'"`\n]+)[\'"`]', content):
    artist_positions.append((m.start(), m.group(1)))

def get_artist_at(pos):
    best = "Unknown"
    for apos, aname in artist_positions:
        if apos <= pos: best = aname
        else: break
    return best

# Find every song-level youtubeId with full context
# A song-level youtubeId is one NOT preceded by "significance" or inside albums:[
song_data = []
for m in re.finditer(r"youtubeId:\s*'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})'", content):
    pos = m.start()
    yt_id = m.group(1)
    # Check if this is inside an album entry (same line has 'significance' or nearby has album markers)
    line_start = content.rfind('\n', 0, pos) + 1
    line_end = content.find('\n', pos)
    line = content[line_start:line_end]
    if 'significance' in line: continue  # album-level
    
    # Scan backward up to 500 chars for id: and title:
    window = content[max(0, pos-600):pos]
    sid_matches = list(re.finditer(r"\n[ \t]+id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", window))
    title_matches = list(re.finditer(r"\n[ \t]+title:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", window))
    
    sid = sid_matches[-1].group(1) if sid_matches else None
    title = title_matches[-1].group(1) if title_matches else None
    aname = get_artist_at(pos)
    
    song_data.append({
        'artist': aname, 'song_id': sid, 'title': title, 'yt_id': yt_id, 'pos': pos
    })

print(f"Total song youtubeIds: {len(song_data)}")

import collections
by_yt = collections.defaultdict(list)
for s in song_data:
    by_yt[s['yt_id']].append(s)

# Build fix targets with full artist+title context
fix_targets = []
for yt_id, songs in sorted(by_yt.items(), key=lambda x: -len(x[1])):
    if len(songs) >= 2:
        for k, s in enumerate(songs):
            if k > 0:
                fix_targets.append(s)

print(f"Songs needing fix: {len(fix_targets)}")
print("\nSample fix targets:")
for s in fix_targets[:20]:
    print(f"  [{s['artist']}] '{s['title']}' ({s['song_id']}) current={s['yt_id']}")

# Save for next step
with open('/tmp/fix_targets.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(fix_targets, f, indent=2)

import re, json, collections

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Build interval map: (start_pos, end_pos, artist_name, artist_id)
# Top-level artist objects start right after "  {\n    id: '" in ARTISTS array
# Find all top-level artist boundaries

# Find ARTISTS array start
arr_start = content.find('export const ARTISTS')

# Find each artist block: starts with "  {\n" at top level of ARTISTS array
# Each artist has "    id: 'xxx'" and "    name: 'xxx'" at 4-space indent
artist_map = []  # (start, name, id)

for m in re.finditer(r"\n  \{\n    id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`][^\n]*\n    name:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", content):
    artist_map.append((m.start(), m.group(1), m.group(2)))

# If that didn't work (mixed indent), try just name with 4-space
if not artist_map:
    for m in re.finditer(r"\n    id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", content):
        if m.start() < arr_start: continue
        # find name nearby
        name_m = re.search(r"name:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", content[m.start():m.start()+200])
        if name_m:
            artist_map.append((m.start(), m.group(1), name_m.group(1)))

print(f"Artist map entries: {len(artist_map)}")
if artist_map:
    print("Sample:", artist_map[:3])

# Check actual indent of artist id
sample = content[arr_start:arr_start+500]
print("\nSample of ARTISTS array:")
print(repr(sample[:300]))

COMMAND:
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import re, json, collections

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

arr_start = content.find('export const ARTISTS')

# Build (pos, artist_id, artist_name) sorted list
artist_map = []
for m in re.finditer(r"\n  \{\n    id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`][^\n]*\n    name:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", content):
    if m.start() >= arr_start:
        artist_map.append((m.start(), m.group(1), m.group(2)))
artist_map.sort()

def get_artist(pos):
    best_id, best_name = "unknown", "Unknown"
    for apos, aid, aname in artist_map:
        if apos <= pos:
            best_id, best_name = aid, aname
        else:
            break
    return best_id, best_name

# Get all song-level youtubeIds with artist context
song_data = []
for m in re.finditer(r"youtubeId:\s*'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})'", content):
    pos = m.start()
    if pos < arr_start: continue
    line_start = content.rfind('\n', 0, pos) + 1
    line_end = content.find('\n', pos)
    line = content[line_start:line_end]
    if 'significance' in line: continue  # album-level

    window = content[max(0, pos-600):pos]
    sid_m = list(re.finditer(r"\n[ \t]+id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", window))
    title_m = list(re.finditer(r"\n[ \t]+title:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", window))
    sid   = sid_m[-1].group(1)   if sid_m   else None
    title = title_m[-1].group(1) if title_m else None
    aid, aname = get_artist(pos)

    song_data.append({'artist_id': aid, 'artist': aname, 'song_id': sid,
                      'title': title, 'yt_id': m.group(1), 'pos': pos})

print(f"Total song youtubeIds: {len(song_data)}")
by_yt = collections.defaultdict(list)
for s in song_data:
    by_yt[s['yt_id']].append(s)

fix_targets = []
print("\n=== All shared IDs (need fix) ===")
for yt_id, songs in sorted(by_yt.items(), key=lambda x: -len(x[1])):
    if len(songs) >= 2:
        for k, s in enumerate(songs):
            if k == 0:
                print(f"\n{yt_id} x{len(songs)}: [KEEP] [{s['artist']}] '{s['title']}' ({s['song_id']})")
            else:
                print(f"  [FIX]  [{s['artist']}] '{s['title']}' ({s['song_id']})")
                fix_targets.append(s)

print(f"\nTotal to fix: {len(fix_targets)}")
with open('/tmp/fix_targets.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(fix_targets, f, indent=2)
print("Saved /tmp/fix_targets.json")

"endIndex": 624, "text": "..." },\n            "groundingChunkIndices": [0, 1, 2]\n          }\n        ],\n        "webSearchQueries": ["Euro 2024 winner"]\n      }\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n### Key INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY\n    ↓\nUpstream SSE streaming response is proxied to the frontend\n    ↓\nFrontend parses the event stream with eventsource-parser\n    ↓\nRender Markdown with streamdown + display source citations\n```\n\n> See `references/ai-search-api.md` for the full parameter table, generation-time code, and Edge Function code.\n\n---\n\n## Generation-Time Usage (Direct Agent accumulate the full text, and return it. The frontend receives the stream using `ky` + `eventsource-parser`, renders the output with `streamdown`, and displays source citation links.\n\n---\n\n## Notes\n\n- **Key security**: `INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY` must only be read server-side inside the Edge Function; never expose it to the frontend.\n- **Source citations are mandatory**: API terms require that when displaying generated content, you **must show** the source URLs obtained via Google Search (`groundingChunks[].web.uri`); omitting them violates the terms of use.\n- **First-token latency**: The first token may take up to 30 seconds; extend the frontend timeout accordingly to avoid false timeout errors.\n- **Streaming required**: The endpoint returns an SSE stream; you must use `EventSource` or an equivalent approach to consume the data — do not use plain `fetch().json()`.\n- **Markdown rendering**: Model output is in Markdown format; it is recommended to use `streamdown@^1.1.6` for streaming rendering.\n- **Error handling**: Always handle 429 (quota exceeded) and 402 (insufficient balance).\n- **Billing**: Discounted price ¥0.19 / call; avoid unnecessary repeated calls.', observation=<ObservationType.SKILL: 'skill'>, skill='ai-search', success=True, data={'object_storage_path': 'skill-aws-online:aws-prod/miaoda_skills/prompts/managed/ai-search/'})

    80 
    81 In the generation-time scenario (direct Agent call), use the following TypeScript code to call the AI Search endpoint, read the SSE stream incrementally, and accumulate the full response text.
    82 
    83 ```typescript
    84 const apiKey = process.env["INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY"]!; // platform_managed key injected by the platform
    85 
    86 interface ContentPart {
    87   text: string;
    88 }
    89 
    90 interface ContentItem {
    91   role: "user" | "model";
    92   parts: ContentPart[];
    93 }
    94 
    95 interface AiSearchResult {
    96   text: string;
    97   sources: Array<{ uri: string; title: string }>;
    98   webSearchQueries: string[];
    99 }
   100 
   101 async function callAiSearch(contents: ContentItem[]): Promise<AiSearchResult> {
   102   const response = await fetch(
   103     "https://app-crlrq8qvf8jl-api-zYm4ze3j7XvL.gateway.appmedo.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:streamGenerateContent?alt=sse",
   104     {
   105       method: "POST",
   106       headers: {
   107         "Content-Type": "application/json",
   108         "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
   109       },
   110       body: JSON.stringify({ contents }),
   111     }
   112   );
   113 
   114   if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP error: ${response.status}`);
   115   if (!response.body) throw new Error("No response body");
   116 
   117   const reader = response.body.getReader();
   118   const decoder = new TextDecoder("utf-8");
   119 
   120   let fullText = "";
   121   const sources: Array<{ uri: string; title: string }> = [];
   122   const webSearchQueries: string[] = [];
   123   let buffer = "";
   124 
   125   while (true) {
   126     const { done, value } = await reader.read();
   127     if (done) break;
   128 
   129     buffer += decoder.decode(value, { stream: true });
   130     const lines = buffer.split("\n");
   131     buffer = lines.pop() ?? "";
   132 
   133     for (const line of lines) {
   134       if (!line.startsWith("data: ")) continue;
   135       const dataStr = line.slice(6).trim();
   136       if (dataStr === "[DONE]") break;
   137       try {
   138         const parsed = JSON.parse(dataStr);
   139         const candidate = parsed?.candidates?.[0];
   140         if (!candidate) continue;
   141 
   142         // Accumulate text
   143         const textChunk = candidate?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text ?? "";
   144         fullText += textChunk;
   145 
   146         // Collect sources (may appear in last chunk)
   147         const meta = candidate?.groundingMetadata;
   148         if (meta) {
   149           for (const chunk of meta.groundingChunks ?? []) {
   150             if (chunk?.web?.uri) {
   151               sources.push({ uri: chunk.web.uri, title: chunk.web.title ?? "" });
   152             }
   153           }
   154           for (const q of meta.webSearchQueries ?? []) {
   155             if (!webSearchQueries.includes(q)) webSearchQueries.push(q);
   156           }
   157         }
   158       } catch {
   159         // Incomplete JSON chunk — skip
   160       }

import re, json, collections

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

arr_start = content.find('export const ARTISTS')
artist_map = []
for m in re.finditer(r"\n  \{\n    id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`][^\n]*\n    name:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", content):
    if m.start() >= arr_start:
        artist_map.append((m.start(), m.group(1), m.group(2)))
artist_map.sort()

def get_artist(pos):
    best_id, best_name = "unknown", "Unknown"
    for apos, aid, aname in artist_map:
        if apos <= pos: best_id, best_name = aid, aname
        else: break
    return best_id, best_name

# Get ALL songs with positions so we can match by position
all_songs = []
# Find each song object: starts with a { and has id, title, youtubeId
for m in re.finditer(r"youtubeId:\s*'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})'", content):
    pos = m.start()
    if pos < arr_start: continue
    line_start = content.rfind('\n', 0, pos) + 1
    line_end = content.find('\n', pos)
    line = content[line_start:line_end]
    if 'significance' in line: continue

    window = content[max(0, pos-800):pos]
    # find song id: look for last id: that is NOT at 4-space (artist level)
    sid_matches = list(re.finditer(r"\n([ \t]{5,})id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", window))
    title_matches = list(re.finditer(r"\n[ \t]+title:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", window))
    sid   = sid_matches[-1].group(2)   if sid_matches   else None
    title = title_matches[-1].group(1) if title_matches else None
    aid, aname = get_artist(pos)

    all_songs.append({'artist_id': aid, 'artist': aname, 'song_id': sid,
                      'title': title, 'yt_id': m.group(1), 'pos': pos})

# Load fix targets
with open('/tmp/fix_targets.json') as f:
    fix_targets = json.load(f)

fix_set = {(s['song_id'], s['yt_id']) for s in fix_targets}

# Get full title for each fix target by matching song_id
song_by_id = {}
for s in all_songs:
    if s['song_id']:
        song_by_id[s['song_id']] = s

print("=== Fix targets with full context ===")
enriched = []
for ft in fix_targets:
    full = song_by_id.get(ft['song_id'], ft)
    enriched.append({
        'artist': full['artist'],
        'artist_id': full['artist_id'],
        'song_id': full['song_id'],
        'title': full['title'],
        'current_yt': ft['yt_id']
    })
    print(f"[{full['artist']}] '{full['title']}' ({full['song_id']})")

with open('/tmp/enriched_targets.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(enriched, f, indent=2)
print(f"\nTotal: {len(enriched)}")

import re, json

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

arr_start = content.find('export const ARTISTS')
artist_map = []
for m in re.finditer(r"\n  \{\n    id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`][^\n]*\n    name:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", content):
    if m.start() >= arr_start:
        artist_map.append((m.start(), m.group(1), m.group(2)))
artist_map.sort()

def get_artist(pos):
    best_id, best_name = "unknown", "Unknown"
    for apos, aid, aname in artist_map:
        if apos <= pos: best_id, best_name = aid, aname
        else: break
    return best_id, best_name

# Find ALL song objects more carefully:
# scan line by line for song objects and capture all fields
songs_full = []
lines = content.split('\n')
i = 0
cur = {}
cur_artist_id, cur_artist_name = None, None
in_songs_section = False

for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    # Track artist
    m = re.match(r'^    id:\s*[\'"`]([^\'"`\n]+)[\'"`]', line)
    if m:
        # check if it's at the artist top level (next line should have name:)
        if i+1 < len(lines) and re.match(r'^    name:', lines[i+1]):
            cur_artist_id = m.group(1)
            in_songs_section = False
    m = re.match(r'^    name:\s*[\'"`]([^\'"`\n]+)[\'"`]', line)
    if m and cur_artist_id:
        cur_artist_name = m.group(1)

    # Detect songs section
    if re.match(r'^    songs:\s*\[', line):
        in_songs_section = True
    if in_songs_section and re.match(r'^    \],', line):
        in_songs_section = False

    if in_songs_section:
        # Song id at 6-space
        ms = re.match(r'^      id:\s*[\'"`]([^\'"`\n]+)[\'"`]', line)
        if ms:
            if cur: songs_full.append(cur)
            cur = {'artist_id': cur_artist_id, 'artist': cur_artist_name,
                   'song_id': ms.group(1), 'title': None, 'yt_id': None}
        mt = re.match(r"^      title:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", line)
        if mt and cur and not cur['title']:
            cur['title'] = mt.group(1)
        my = re.match(r"^      youtubeId:\s*'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})'", line)
        if my and cur and not cur['yt_id']:
            cur['yt_id'] = my.group(1)
            songs_full.append(cur)
            cur = {}

if cur and cur.get('yt_id'): songs_full.append(cur)

print(f"Songs with full data: {len(songs_full)}")
by_sid = {s['song_id']: s for s in songs_full if s['song_id']}
print(f"Unique song IDs: {len(by_sid)}")
print("Sample:", list(by_sid.values())[:3])
with open('/tmp/songs_full.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(songs_full, f, indent=2)

python3 << 'PYEOF'
import re, json, subprocess

with open('/workspace/app-crlrq8qvf8jl/src/data/artists.ts', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

arr_start = content.find('export const ARTISTS')

# Build artist pos map
artist_map = []
for m in re.finditer(r"\n  \{\n    id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`][^\n]*\n    name:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", content):
    if m.start() >= arr_start:
        artist_map.append((m.start(), m.group(1), m.group(2)))
artist_map.sort()

def get_artist(pos):
    best_id, best_name = "unknown", "Unknown"
    for apos, aid, aname in artist_map:
        if apos <= pos: best_id, best_name = aid, aname
        else: break
    return best_id, best_name

# Find each youtubeId occurrence and scan BACKWARD more broadly for the song data
# Scan up to 1200 chars to catch multi-line template literal songs
results = []
for m in re.finditer(r"youtubeId:\s*'([A-Za-z0-9_\-]{11})'", content):
    pos = m.start()
    if pos < arr_start: continue
    line_s = content.rfind('\n', 0, pos) + 1
    line_e = content.find('\n', pos)
    if 'significance' in content[line_s:line_e]: continue

    # Wider backward scan
    window = content[max(0, pos-1500):pos]
    
    # Find all id: occurrences (skip artist-level at 4-space)
    sid_matches = list(re.finditer(r"\n([ \t]{5,})id:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", window))
    title_matches = list(re.finditer(r"\n[ \t]+title:\s*['\"`]([^'\"`\n]+)['\"`]", window))
    
    sid   = sid_matches[-1].group(2)   if sid_matches   else None
    title = title_matches[-1].group(1) if title_matches else None
    aid, aname = get_artist(pos)

    results.append({'artist_id': aid, 'artist': aname, 'song_id': sid,
                    'title': title, 'yt_id': m.group(1), 'pos': pos})

print(f"Total song youtubeIds: {len(results)}")

import collections
by_yt = collections.defaultdict(list)
for s in results:
    by_yt[s['yt_id']].append(s)

fix_targets = []
for yt_id, songs in sorted(by_yt.items(), key=lambda x: -len(x[1])):
    if len(songs) >= 2:
        for k, s in enumerate(songs):
            if k > 0:
                fix_targets.append(s)

none_count = sum(1 for s in fix_targets if s['title'] is None)
print(f"Fix targets: {len(fix_targets)}, with None title: {none_count}")

# For None titles, derive from song_id
def title_from_id(sid):
    if not sid: return None
    return ' '.join(w.capitalize() for w in sid.replace('-', ' ').split())

for s in fix_targets:
    if s['title'] is None and s['song_id']:
        s['title'] = title_from_id(s['song_id'])
    # Also mark ones we still can't resolve
    if s['title'] is None:
        s['title'] = f"[unknown-{s['song_id']}]"

print("\n=== Enriched targets ===")
for s in fix_targets:
    print(f"  [{s['artist']}] '{s['title']}' ({s['song_id']})")

with open('/tmp/fix_targets_enriched.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(fix_targets, f, indent=2)

import urllib.request, json, os, sys, time

API_KEY = os.environ.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY", "")
ENDPOINT = "https://app-crlrq8qvf8jl-api-zYm4ze3j7XvL.gateway.appmedo.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:streamGenerateContent?alt=sse"

def search(query):
    body = json.dumps({"contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": query}]}]}).encode()
    req = urllib.request.Request(ENDPOINT, data=body, method="POST",
        headers={"Content-Type": "application/json",
                 "X-Gateway-Authorization": f"Bearer {API_KEY}"})
    try:
        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=60) as resp:
            full = ""
            for line in resp:
                line = line.decode('utf-8').strip()
                if not line.startswith("data: "): continue
                data = line[6:].strip()
                if data == "[DONE]": break
                try:
                    p = json.loads(data)
                    t = p.get("candidates", [{}])[0].get("content", {}).get("parts", [{}])[0].get("text", "")
                    full += t
                except: pass
            return full.strip()
    except Exception as e:
        return f"ERROR: {e}"

if __name__ == "__main__":
    query = sys.argv[1]
    result = search(query)
    print(result)
EOF

     1 # Dokumen Persyaratan
     2 
     3 ## 1. Ikhtisar Aplikasi
     4 
     5 **Nama Aplikasi**: Trip-Hop Archive Map
     6 
     7 **Deskripsi**: Peta musik interaktif berbasis web dan timeline yang mendokumentasikan evolusi genre Trip-Hop dari akhir 1980-an hingga saat ini. Aplikasi ini berfungsi sebagai arsip hidup dan museum sonik dengan estetika underground tahun 90-an, menampilkan node artis yang dapat dijelajahi, konteks historis, integrasi multimedia, dan manajemen playlist dengan kemampuan ekspor ke Spotify.
     8 
     9 ## 2. Pengguna dan Kasus Penggunaan
    10 
    11 **Pengguna Target**:
    12 - Sejarawan musik dan peneliti
    13 - Penggemar dan kolektor trip-hop
    14 - Penjelajah budaya musik underground
    15 - Mahasiswa musik yang mempelajari evolusi genre
    16 
    17 **Kasus Penggunaan Inti**:
    18 - Menjelajahi asal-usul dan evolusi genre Trip-Hop
    19 - Menemukan koneksi dan pengaruh antar artis
    20 - Meneliti konteks historis album dan track
    21 - Menemukan artis serupa dan rilis tersembunyi
    22 - Membuat dan mengelola playlist pribadi
    23 - Mengekspor playlist ke Spotify
    24 - Mengakses playlist tematik yang dikurasi
    25 - Membagikan playlist pribadi dengan orang lain
    26 - Menelusuri dan menemukan lagu di semua artis
    27 - Memfilter dan mencari lagu berdasarkan mood, era, judul, atau artis
    28 
    29 ## 3. Struktur Halaman dan Deskripsi Fungsional
    30 
    31 ```
    32 Trip-Hop Archive Map
    33 ├── Main Map Canvas
    34 │   ├── Origins Node (1980s-1992)
    35 │   ├── Golden Age Node (1993-1999)
    36 │   ├── Expansion Node (2000-2010)

   276 - Menerapkan perlakuan fotografi cahaya rendah
   277 - Menyertakan tekstur Xerox dan artefak offset printing
   278 - Menerapkan pemrosesan gambar monokrom dengan efek cahaya biru
   279 
   280 **Pemrosesan Cover Album**:
   281 - Mengonversi semua cover album ke versi terindeks monokrom biru
   282 - Menerapkan posterisasi dan dithering
   283 - Mempertahankan pengenalan sambil mencapai estetika arsip
   284 
   285 **Pemrosesan Gambar Artis**:
   286 - Mengambil gambar artis dari URL nyata (cover album atau foto artis)
   287 - Menerapkan CSS filter: sepia(1) hue-rotate(190deg) saturate(2) brightness(0.65)
   288 - Merender sebagai thumbnail melingkar yang dipotong dalam lingkaran node artis canvas
   289 - Gambar sesuai dengan estetika arsip monokrom biru tua
   290 
   291 ### 4.2 Aturan Animasi
   292 
   293 **Pergerakan Kamera**:
   294 - Pergerakan inersia halus dengan momentum
   295 - Transisi zoom dengan efek blur-to-focus
   296 - Parallax ambient lambat untuk elemen background
   297 
   298 **Perilaku Node**:
   299 - Simulasi fisika drift halus
   300 - Hover memicu efek reaktif noise
   301 - Klik memicu animasi ekspansi
   302 
   303 **Transisi**:
   304 - Transisi pixelated antar tampilan
   305 - Overlay glitch VHS pada perubahan state
   306 - Efek gerakan cairan
   307 
   308 **Animasi Background**:
   309 - Visual abstrak atmosferik berkelanjutan
   310 - Partikel reaktif audio saat musik diputar

   317 - Tipis: koneksi scene/era

   320 - Warna atau tingkat opacity yang berbeda membedakan:

   351 
   352 **Algoritma Discover Similar**:

   357 ### 4.7 Aturan Manajemen Playlist
   358 
   359 **Add to Playlist**:
   360 - Pengguna mengklik tombol Add to Playlist pada lagu apa pun
   361 - Lagu ditambahkan ke akhir antrian playlist pribadi
   362 - Lagu duplikat diperbolehkan
   363 
   364 **Ekspor Playlist**:
   365 - Export as YouTube Playlist Link menghasilkan URL yang dapat dibagikan dengan semua link YouTube
   366 - Copy as Text memformat playlist sebagai: Judul Lagu - Nama Artis (Link YouTube) satu per baris
   367 
   368 **Bagikan Playlist**:
   369 - Encode playlist pribadi sebagai string JSON base64 terkompresi
   370 - Tambahkan string yang di-encode ke hash URL (#playlist=...)
   371 - Klik tombol Share Playlist menyalin URL lengkap ke clipboard
   372 - Saat loading halaman, deteksi parameter playlist di hash URL
   373 - Decode hash dan pre-populate playlist
   374 
   375 **Ekspor Spotify**:
   376 - Pengguna mengklik tombol Export to Spotify
   377 - Memulai alur Spotify OAuth PKCE
   378 - Redirect ke halaman otorisasi Spotify dengan scope yang diperlukan: playlist-modify-public, playlist-modify-private
   379 - Setelah pengguna mengotorisasi, Spotify redirect kembali dengan kode otorisasi
   380 - Tukar kode untuk access token
   381 - Membuat playlist Spotify baru melalui Spotify Web API
   382 - Untuk setiap lagu dalam playlist pribadi, cari Spotify berdasarkan judul + artis
   383 - Tambahkan track yang ditemukan ke playlist yang dibuat
   384 - Menampilkan pesan sukses dengan link ke playlist Spotify
   385 - Menangani error: kegagalan otorisasi, kegagalan pencarian, error API
   386 
   387 **Perilaku Playlist Terkurasi**:
   388 - Playlist yang telah dibuat sebelumnya bersifat read-only
   389 - Pengguna dapat menambahkan seluruh playlist terkurasi ke playlist pribadi
   390 - Pengguna dapat menambahkan lagu individual dari playlist terkurasi ke playlist pribadi

   259                           <span className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 w-3 h-3 bg-accent text-background text-center font-mono leading-3 rounded-full" style={{ fontSize: '0.45rem' }}>
   260                             {playlistQueue.length > 9 ? '9+' : playlistQueue.length}
   261                           </span>
   262                         )}
   263                       </div>
   264                     ),
   265                     label: 'LIST',
   266                     panel: 'playlist' as RightPanel,
   267                   },
   268                 ] as Array<{ icon: React.ReactNode; label: string; panel: RightPanel; disabled?: boolean }>).map(({ icon, label, panel, disabled }) => (
   269                   <button
   270                     key={label}
   271                     onClick={() => !disabled && openPanel(panel)}
   272                     disabled={disabled}
   273                     className={`flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 xerox-border text-xs font-mono transition-all ${
   274                       rightPanel === panel
   275                         ? 'border-accent text-accent bg-accent/10'
   276                         : disabled
   277                           ? 'opacity-30 cursor-not-allowed border-border text-muted-foreground'
   278                           : 'border-border text-muted-foreground hover:border-accent/50 hover:text-foreground'
   279                     }`}
   280                     title={disabled ? 'Select an artist first' : undefined}
   281                   >
   282                     {icon}
   283                     <span className="hidden md:inline">{label}</span>
   284                   </button>
   285                 ))}
   286 
   287                 <button
   288                   onClick={toggleAudio}
   289                   className="flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 xerox-border text-xs font-mono border-border text-muted-foreground hover:border-accent/50 hover:text-foreground transition-all"
   290                 >
   291                   {audioEnabled ? <Volume2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> : <VolumeX className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />}
   292                 </button>
   293               </div>
   294             </div>
   295 
   296             {/* BODY */}
   297             <div className="flex-1 flex overflow-hidden min-h-0">
   298               {/* LEFT SIDEBAR */}
   299               {!sidebarCollapsed && (
   300                 <div className="flex-shrink-0 w-52 border-r border-border bg-background/60 backdrop-blur-sm z-20 overflow-y-auto flex flex-col">
   301                   <div className="p-3 flex-1 space-y-5">
   302                     <TimelineScrubber yearRange={yearRange} onYearRangeChange={setYearRange} activeEra={activeEra} onEraChange={handleEraChange} />

   305

   308                       <div className="text-lg font-bold font-mono text-accent text-glow">{visibleCount}</div>
   309                       <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">of {ARTISTS.length} total</div>
   310                     </div>
   311 
   312                     {similarArtists.length > 0 && (
   313                       <div className="border-t border-border pt-3">
   314                         <div className="archival-label mb-2 flex items-center gap-1">

   316                         </div>

   327                           ))}
   328                         </div>
   329                       </div>
   330                     )}
   331                   </div>
   332                   <div className="p-3 border-t border-border">

   334                   </div>
   335                 </div>
   336               )}
   337

   339               <div className="flex-1 relative min-w-0 overflow-hidden">
   340                 <GenreMapCanvas
   341                   activeMoods={activeMoods}
   342                   activeEra={activeEra}
   343                   yearRange={yearRange}
   344                   onSelectArtist={handleSelectArtist}
   345                   selectedArtistId={selectedArtist?.id ?? null}
   346                 />
   347               </div>
   348

   350               {rightPanel && (

   352                   {rightPanel === 'artist' && selectedArtist && (
   353                     <ArtistPanel

   374                         if (a) handleSelectArtist(a);
   375                       }}
   376                     />
   377                   )}
   378                   {rightPanel === 'dna' && selectedArtist && (
   379                     <SoundDNA artist={selectedArtist} onClose={() => setRightPanel(null)} />
   380                   )}

   383                   )}

   401                     <SongsDiscovery
   402                       onClose={() => setRightPanel(null)}
   403                       onAddToPlaylist={handleAddToPlaylist}
   404                       onSelectSong={entry => {
   405                         const artist = ARTISTS.find(a => a.id === entry.artistId);

   409                           setSelectedSong(song);
   410                           setRightPanel('song');
   411                         }
   412                       }}
   413                     />
   414                   )}
   415                   {rightPanel === 'wiki' && (
   416                     <WikiPanel onClose={() => setRightPanel(null)} />
   417                   )}
   418                   {rightPanel === 'audit' && (
   419                     <YouTubeAuditPanel onClose={() => setRightPanel(null)} />
   420                   )}
   421                 </div>
   422               )}
   423             </div>
